9a2('bum): 'das de ltar sled pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// bsam gtaran gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i
9a3('bum): tshul gyis slong // brjer 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ bzed pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin
9a4('bum): pa la ri dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
9a5('bum): sleng po/ yang dag par spong ba rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la mi dmigs nga'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ dbang po rnams la mi dmigs
9a6('bum): pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ stobs rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la
9a7('bum): mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul d+hisu sleb bo// bsam gtan rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo// tshad med pa rnams la
9a8('bum): mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo// gzugs meng pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slong bo/ rnam par thar pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slong ba/ mthar
9b1('bum): gyis gnas pa'i sems par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / sdod pa med pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul
9b2('bum): gyis sleb bo/ mngon par shes pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo// ting nge 'dzin rnams la mi dmigs pa'i rdul gyis slob bo/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul
9b3('bum): gyis sleb bo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo/ mi 'jigs pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ so so yang dag par rig pa
9b4('bum): rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo// byams pa chen po la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob bo// snying rje chen po la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sbeng po/ sangs rgyas kyi
9b5('bum): chos pa 'dres pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb bo/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA radwa ti'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ 
9b6('bum): de ltar sleb pa ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ brjom grus kyi
9b7('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yis bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
9b8('bum): sleb pa yin/ sbyir pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yid/ yang dag par spong ba
10a1('bum): mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la mi darigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ dbang po rnams la mi darigs pa'i rdul gyis slob pa yin
10a2('bum): sdebs rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul
10a3('bum): gyis slob pa yin/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ bsam gtan rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ tshad med pa rnams la mi rigra
10a4('bum): pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ rnam par thar pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
10a5('bum): sleb pa yin/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yid/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / 
10a6('bum): sper pa med pa la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ mngon par shes pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ 
10a7('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la mi darigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ mi 'jigs pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i
10a8('bum): tshul gyis slob pa yin/ so so yang dag par rig pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ byams pa chen po la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin/ seng rje chen po la mi dmis
10b1('bum): pa'i tshul gyis slob pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams la mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis sleb pa yin no// shA radwa ti'i bus gsel ba/ bcom ldan 'das ci'i srang du mi darigs pa lags
10b2('bum): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir bdag mi dmigs so// / sems can mi dmigs so// 'gro ba ri rig so// gso ba mi dmig so// 
10b3('bum): skyes bu mi dmigs so// gang zag mi dmig so// shed can mi dmig so// shed bdag mi dmigs so// byed pa po mi dmigs so// tshor ba po mi dmigs so// shes pa po mi dmigs
10b4('bum): mthong ba po mi dmigs// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir gzugs mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir tshor ba mi dmigaso// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ 'ang
10b5('bum): shes mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ 'du byed mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rnam par shes pa mi dmig so// shir tu rnam pa
10b6('bum): dag pa'i phyir/ rig mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rna ba mi dmigaso// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ sna mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir
10b7('bum): lde mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ lus mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ yid mi dmigs// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ gzugs mi

11a3('bum): pa'i phyir/ rna ba'i khams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ sgra'i khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i khams mi

11a7('bum): phyir/ reg gi khams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ yid kyi khams mi dmigaso/ 
11a8('bum): shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ chos kyi khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir
11b1('bum): sa'i khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ chu'i khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ me'i khams mi dmig sa// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rlung gi
11b2('bum): khams mi darigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ na mkha'i khams mi dmigs// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rnam par shes pa'i khams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag

11b8('bum): dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ 'dod pa'i khams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ gzugs kyi khams mi dmigs so// shir tu dam par dag pa'i phyir/ garda

12a7('bum): pa rnams mi dmigs// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ bsam gtan rnams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ tshad med pa rnams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/

12b1('bum): sems par 'jug pa rnams mi dmigs so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag
12b2('bum): pa'i phyir/ mngon par shes pa rnams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ ting nge 'dzin rnams mi dmig so// shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams mi dmigs so//

13a3('bum): bcom ldan 'das de ltar slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ chos gang dang gang la slob pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA radwa ti'i bu de

13a5('bum): ji ltar mngon par chags par bya ba de lta bu rnam par yo dpa ma yin no// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'o/ na chos 'di dag rnam pa gang gis mchis pa lags/ bcom

84b1('bum): rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ nam rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'id dang ldan pa'i yid la bya bas/ rnam pa 'ji
84b2('bum): rab tu rdzogs te gzugs kyi stong pa nyid kyis gzugs stong pa ma yin gyi gzugs nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang gzugs so// tshor ba'i stong pa nyid kyis tshor ba steng pa ma yin gyi tshor ba
84b3('bum): kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang tshor ba'o// 'du shes kyi stong pa nyid kyis 'du shes stong pa ma yin gyi 'du shes nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang 'du sheso// 'du byed kyi stong pa nyid kyis
84b4('bum): 'du byed stong pa ma yin gyi/ 'du byed med kyang stong pa nyid ngo // stong panyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis rnam par shes pa sdong pa ma yin gyi rnam par shes pa
84b5('bum): nyi kyang steng pa'i ngo // sdong pa'i kyang rnam par shes pa'o// mig gi stong pa nyid kyis mig stong pa ma yin gyi mig nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // stong pa nyid kyang mig go// rna ba'i stong pa
84b6('bum): nyid kyis rna ba stong pa ma yin gyi rna banyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong panyid kyang rna ba'o// sna'i stong pa nyid kyis sna stong pa ma yin gyi sna nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // stong pa nyid kyang snga'o// lce'i stong panyid
84b7('bum): kyis lde sbeng pa ma yin gyi lce nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // stong pa'i kyang lde'o// lus kyi stong pa nyid kyis lus stong pa ma yin gyi lus nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa'id kyang lus so// yid kyi steng pa'i
84b8('bum): kyis yid steng pa ma yin gyi yid nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // stong pa nyid kyang yid do// gzugs kyi steng pa nyid kyis gzugs stong pa ma yin gyi gzugs nyid kyang stong pa'id ngo // steng pa nyid kyang gzug sa
85a1('bum): sgra'i steng shing kyi sgra steng pa ma yin gyi sgra nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa'i kyang sgra'o// dri'i steng pa nyid kyis dri steng pa ma yin gyi dri'i kyang steng pa'ing ngo // steng shing kyang dri'o// 
85a2('bum): re'i stong pa nyid kyis re steng pa ma yin gyi re nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo do// stong panyid kyang ro'o// reg gi stong pa nyid kyis reg steng pa ma yin gyi gnyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // steng panyid kyang reg go// chos kyi stong pa
85a3('bum): nyid kyis chos stong pa ma yin gyi chos nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang chos so// mig gi rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis mig gi rnam par shes pa steng pa ma yin gyi mig gi rnam par shes pa'id
85a4('bum): kyang sdong pa'id ngo // stong pa'i kyang mig gi rnam par shes pa'o// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis rna ba'i rnam par shes pa stong pa ma yin gyi rna ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang stong
85a5('bum): pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o// sna'i rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis sna'i rnam par shes pa ste/ nga ba ma yin gyi sna'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang ster ba'ing ngo // 
85a6('bum): stong pa nyid kyang sna'i rnam par shes pa'o// lce'i rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis lce'i rnam par shes pa steng pa ma yin gyi lce'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// steng pa nyid kyang lce'i rnam par shes
85a7('bum): pa'o// lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis lus kyi rnam par shes pa stong pa ma yin gyi lus kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o// yid
85a8('bum): kyi rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis yid kyi rnam par shes pa stong pa ma yin gyi yid kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i sngang
85b1('bum): pa'i da kyis mig gi 'dus te reg pa steng pa ma yin gyi mig gi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i steng pa nyid kyis rna ba'i 'dus te reg
85b2('bum): pa stong pa ma yin gyi rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i steng pa nyid kyis sna'i 'dus te reg pa stong pa ma yin gyi sna'i 'dus te
85b3('bum): reg pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang sna'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid kyis lce'i 'dus te reg pa stong pa ma yin gyi lce'i 'dus te reg panyid kyang stong pa nyid do// 
85b4('bum): stong pa nyid kyang lde'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid kyis lus kyi 'dus te reg pa stong pa ma yin gyi lus kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa
85b5('bum): nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid kyis yid kyi 'dus te reg pa stong pa ma yin gyi yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i dkyang stong pa'i ngo // stong pa
85b6('bum): nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i stong pa nyid kyis mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba stong pa ma yin gyi mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tsher
85b7('bum): yi kyang stong pa'ing ngo // stong pa nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i stong pa nyid kyis rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor bsdu
85b8('bum): pa ma yin gyi rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang steng pa nyid ngo // stong panyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor ba'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rgyar gyis dor ba'i stong pa'i
86a1('bum): kyis snga'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba stong pa ma yin gyi sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'id kyang sdong pa'i ngo // stong pa'id kyang sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen
86a2('bum): gyis tshor ba'o// lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i stong pa nyid kyis lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba stong pa ma yin gyi lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang steng pa nyid do// steng
86a3('bum): pa'i dkyang lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba steng pa nyid kyis lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor bsteng pa ma yin gyi lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i
86a4('bum): rkyer gyis tshor ba'i kyang steng pa nyid ngo // stong pa nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i stong pa'i dkyis yid
86a5('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor bstong pa ma yin gyi yid kyi 'du sa te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang stong pa'i ngo // stong panyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg lnga 'i rkyer gyis tshor ba'o/ 
86a6('bum): sa'i khams kyi stong pa nyid kyis sa'i khams stong pa ma yin gyi sa'i khams nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang sa'i khams so// chu'i khams kyi stong panyid kyis chu'i khams steng ba ma yin gyi chu'i kham
86a7('bum): nyid kyang steng pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang chu'i kham so// me'i khams kyi stong pa nyid kyis me'i khams stong pa ma yin gyi me'i khams nyid kyang steng pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang me'i kham so// rlung gi
86a8('bum): khams kyi stong pa nyid kyis rlung gi khams stong pa ma yin gyi rlung gi khams nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang rlung gi khamaso// namakha'i khams kyi stong pa nyid kyis rnam pa'i khams stong pa ma yin gyi
86b1('bum): namakha'i khams nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang na mkha'i khams so// rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi stong pa nyid kyis rnam par shes pa'i khams stong par yin gyi rnam par shes pa'i khams nyid
86b2('bum): kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'i kham so// ma rig pa'i stong pa nyid kyis ma rig pa stong pa pa yin gyi ma rig pa'i dkyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang ma rig pa'o// 'du byed
86b3('bum): kyi stong pa nyid kyis 'du byed stong pa ma yin gyi 'du byed nyid kyang stong pa nyid ngo do// stong pa nyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid kyis rnam par shes pa stong pa ma yin gyi rnam par shes

87a2('bum): sdong pa ma yin gyi/ rga shi nying kyang stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid kyang rga shi'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i stong nyid kyis sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa stong pa ma yid gyi/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa

87b1('bum): sdong pa'i dkyis/ nang stong pa 'ing stong pas yin gyi/ nang stong pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// stong panyid kyang nang stong pa nyid do// phyi stong pa nyid kyi steng pa nyid kyis phyi stong pa nyid stong pa ma yin gyi/ byi stong

88a1('bum): / yid kyis theg sa dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid stong pa ma yin gyi/ thog pa dang tha med pa stong pa nyid kyang stong pa nyid do// steng panyid kyang thog ma dang tham med pa steng pa'i dang

90a1('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ rab 'byor 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa

121b3('bum): par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhi zhes bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos sten cing / dge ba'i

157b5('bum): ces bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams cad ma khye/ pa nyid ma rtogs par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar
157b6('bum): yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la sangs rgyas kyi chos pa 'dres pa rnams smon pa med ces bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyer pa
157b7('bum): nyid ma rtogs par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams mngon par 'du bya ba med ces bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul
157b8('bum): gyis chos ston cing dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ma rtogs par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la sangs rgyas
158a1('bum): chos ma 'dres pa rnams dben des bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ma rtogs par
158a2('bum): thos kyi sa 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi sar yong su sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams bsgom pa'i phyir de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad
158a3('bum): kyang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ma rtogs par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// gang de la rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'ing bsgom pa'i phyir de mi
158a4('bum): dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams mkhyen pa nyid ma rtogs par nyan thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// 
158a5('bum): gang de la byang chub bsgom pa'i phyir/ de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos ston cing / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nying pa rtogs par
158a6('bum): thos kyi sa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yongasu sngor mi 'jug pa'o// // shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa
158a7('bum): rab 'byor 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen du shes par byas te/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen nges yongasu zin pa'i byang chub
158a8('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di thos na mi 'jigs mi sdang skrag par mi 'gyur ro// rab 'byor gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar
158b1('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa 'di thos na/ 'jigs shing sdang la skrag par 'gyur zhing
158b2('bum): thabs mi mkhas te/ sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu lhung zhing dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongasu spangs pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor 'di la byang chub
158b3('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i cha/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom zhing
158b4('bum): dmigs te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa des rlom sems su byed pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par bas pa gdan gyi pha rol tu phyin
158b5('bum): pa bsgom zhing dmigs te/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa des rlob semasu byed pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par brjod 'grus
158b6('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom zhing dmigs te/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa des rlom semasu byed pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par bzed pa'i pha rol tu
158b7('bum): phyin pa bsgom zhing dmigs te/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa des rlob semasu byed pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom
158b8('bum): zhing dmigs te/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa des rlom semasu byed pa dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom ning dmigs
159a1('bum): sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa des rlom sems byed do// de lta bu ni rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i thabs
159a2('bum): mi mkhas par rig par bya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la
159a3('bum): bya ba med par/ gzugs nang stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de// dmigs pa'i tshul gyis nang stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pa'o
159a4('bum): tuphyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs phyi stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis phyi stong
159a5('bum): pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlob sems su byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i che/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya
159a6('bum): ba med par/ gzugs phyi nang stong pa nyid zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyi kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol
159a7('bum): tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs stong pa nyid stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis stong pa nyid stong pa nyid
159a8('bum): kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ gzugs
159b1('bum): chen po stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chen po stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod
159b2('bum): pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs don dam pa stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang dmigs
159b3('bum): la stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom sems byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs 'dus byas

159b5('bum): pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ gzugs 'dus ma byas stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
159b6('bum): 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa
159b7('bum): nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs mtha' las 'das pa stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la
159b8('bum): stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs thog ma dang tha ma med
160a1('bum): pa stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom sems byed do// 
160a2('bum): de shesar gyi pha ral 'phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs dor ba med pa steng pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis

160a4('bum): par/ gzugs rang bzhin stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang dmig sa la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlob semasu byed de// de shes ra

160a7('bum): ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ gzugs rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlob sems
160a8('bum): su byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par gzugs mi dmigs pa stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de

160b2('bum): pa nyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ gzugs dngos po med pa med pa steng pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa

161b8('bum): bdin sbed pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la snga

163b2('bum): la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis dor ba med pa stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams

163b5('bum): yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cang stong pa nyid kyang dmigs la/ stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin

222a4('bum): la bya ba med par/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba chos thams cad stong pa zhes bya bar yid la byed de/ dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad sdong pa'i dkyang dmig
222a5('bum): la stong pa nyid kyis kyang rlom semasu byed do// de shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen panyid dang ldan pa'i yid la bya ba med par/ yid kyi

274b5('bum): ro// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu gzu gas med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na smra ba'i sa
274b6('bum): bu rnam par thar pa brgyad la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor
274b7('bum): 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na sgyu ma'i skyes bu mngon
274b8('bum): par shes pa rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu ting nge 'dzin rnams la spyod pa'i tshig don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu
275a1('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub
275a2('bum): sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes
275a3('bum): bu mi 'jigs pa rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na sgyu ma'i skyes bu so so yang dag par rig pa rnams la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na sna
275a4('bum): ma'i skyes bu byams pa che na la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu snying rje chen bol spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper
275a5('bum): na sgyu ma'i skyes bu sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la spyod pa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha
275a6('bum): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gzugs la gnas

299a5('bum): rnams skye ba med pa la gnas med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams 'gag pa med pa la gnas med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang
299a6('bum): rnam par byang ba med pa la gnas med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la gnas med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// 
299a7('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams mi dmigs pa la gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams skye ba med pa la gnas med do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
299a8('bum): rnams 'gag pa med pa la gnas med do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa la gnas med do// 
299b1('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la gnas med do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// de bzhin
299b2('bum): gshegs pa'i stobs rnams mi dmigs pa la gnas med do// rab 'byor mi 'jigs pa rnams skye ba med pa la gnas med do// mi 'jigs pa rnams 'gag pa
299b3('bum): la gnas med do// mi 'jigs pa rnams kun nas 'on mongs pa med pa dang rnam par byang ba med pa la gnas med do// ri 'jigs pa rnams
299b4('bum): mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la gnas med do// mi 'jigs pa rnams 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// mi 'jigs pa rnams mi dmigs pal
299b5('bum): gnas med do// rab 'byor so so yang dag par rig pa rnams skye ba med pa la gnas med do// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams 'gag pa med pa la
299b6('bum): gnas med do// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa la gnas med do// so so yang dag par rig
299b7('bum): nga rnams mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la gnas med do// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams mi
299b8('bum): dmigs pa la gnas med do// rab 'byor byams pa chen po skye ba med pa la gnas med do// byams pa chen po 'gag pa med pa la gnas med do// byams pa chen

300a2('bum): gnas med do// byams pa chen po 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// byams pa chen po mi dmigs pa la gnas med do// rab 'byor snying rje chen po skye ba med pa

300a4('bum): snying rje chen po mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la gnas med do// snying rje chen po 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// snying rje chen po mi dmigs pa la gnas med do// 
300a5('bum): rab 'byor sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams skye ba med pa la gnas med do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dre sa pa rnams 'gag pa med pa la gnas med do// 
300a6('bum): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa la gnas med do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams mngon par 'du bya ba med
300a7('bum): pa la gnas med do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams 'byung ba med pa la gnas med do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams mi dmigs pa la gnas med
300a8('bum): rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ gzugs shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas
300b1('bum): med do// 'du shes shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 'du byed shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rnam par shes pa shin tu rna
300b2('bum): par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi
300b3('bum): don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ mig shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rna ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
300b4('bum): sna shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lce shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas me dado// lus shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtsha
300b5('bum): ma'i gnas med do// yid shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
300b6('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ gzugs shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
300b7('bum): sgra shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// dri shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// ro shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
300b8('bum): rig shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// chos shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems
301a1('bum): chen po shes rab kyi pha rob tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lnga ste dper na/ mig gi rnam par
301a2('bum): shes pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan pa'i gnas med do// sna'i rnam par shes pa shin tu rnam par
301a3('bum): dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lce'i rnam par shes pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lus kyi rnam par shes pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i
301a4('bum): gnas med do// yid kyi rnam par shes pa shin tu rnam bar dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
301a5('bum): po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam
301a6('bum): par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// sna'i 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan pa'i
301a7('bum): gnas med do// lce'i 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
301a8('bum): yid kyi 'dus te reg pa shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub
301b1('bum): sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rna ba'i 'dus
301b2('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lde'i 'dus
301b3('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// yid
301b4('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba shin tu rnam par dag pa la mchin ma'i gnas med do// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol
301b5('bum): phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med do// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sa'i khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
301b6('bum): chu'i khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// me'i khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rlung gi khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan
301b7('bum): ma'i gnas med do// namakha'i khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// rnam par shes pa'i khams shin tu rnam par dag pa la mtshan ma'i gnas med do// 
301b8('bum): 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gi don med de// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ ma rig pa shin
